        <p>
         Though there was a time when
         <a data-track="Body Text Link: Internal: thecut" href="http://nymag.com/thecut/2010/01/affronts_to_nature_jimmy_choo.html">
          Jimmy Choo x Uggs
         </a>
         were
         <a data-track="Body Text Link: External" href="http://www.upscalehype.com/2011/01/megan-fox-vs-kim-kardashian-in-jimmy-choo-x-ugg-mandah-boots/">
          her cozy shoes
         </a>
         of choice, it appears that Kim Kardashian has upgraded her preferences in fuzzy footwear. Last night, she enjoyed dinner with Kanye in Brentwood while resting her feet on luscious tufts of rabbit fur, courtesy of
         <a data-track="Body Text Link: Internal: thecut" href="http://nymag.com/thecut/fashion/designers/celine/">
          Cline
         </a>
         . She paired the fur-lined stiletto sandals  previously
         <a data-track="Body Text Link: External" href="http://www.stylebistro.com/Industry+Spotlight/articles/cYkCYDsvImA/Celine+Phoebe+Philo+Wins+Designer+Year+Rabbit">
          seen on Phoebe Philo
         </a>
         herself  with a dusty purple mock turtleneck and knit black pencil skirt for a furry take on
         <a data-track="Body Text Link: Internal: thecut" href="http://nymag.com/thecut/2012/08/kim-kardashian-look-book.html">
          her usual look
         </a>
         .
        </p>
